Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1144, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 271. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 126

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 99 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 29 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 33 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 81

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r3, score 48 (Element id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package axe, test duplicate-id, score 6 (id attribute value is not unique)
  • Package continuum, test 94, score 48 (Element contains an id attribute set to a value that is not unique in the DOM)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_1.F77, score 24 (Duplicate id attribute value)

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 78

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 58 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 13 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 32 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 78

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 31 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 36 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 8 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package ibm, test IBMA_Color_Contrast_WCAG2AA, score 28 (Contrast ratio of text with background does not meet WCAG 2.1 AA)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 33 (Very low contrast)
